toggle_county_commerce = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = {

			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_1_exotics_g

			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_exotics_g

			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_0_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_0_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_1_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_1_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_1_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_2_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_2_tools
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_price_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_0_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_0_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_0_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_1_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_1_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_1_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_2_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_armaments
			remove_variable = toggle_county_commerce_scope_2_armaments
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_commerce
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_food
				value = county.var:trade_price_food
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_cereal
				value = county.var:trade_price_cereal
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_salted
				value = county.var:trade_price_salted
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_salt
				value = county.var:trade_price_salt
			}

				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_mud
				value = county.var:trade_price_mud
			}

				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_fuel
				value = county.var:trade_price_fuel
			}

				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_fiber

				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_exotics_e
				value = county.var:trade_price_exotics_e
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_exotics_g
				value = county.var:trade_price_exotics_g
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_textile
				value = county.var:trade_price_textile
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_pottery
				value = county.var:trade_price_pottery
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_tools
				value = county.var:trade_price_tools
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_price_armaments
				value = county.var:trade_price_armaments
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = toggle_county_commerce_t
			county = { 
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = trade_dat_food
					scope:toggle_county_commerce_t = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = toggle_county_commerce_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = array_trade_dat_food
					scope:toggle_county_commerce_t = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_abs_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_abs_tt
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_abs_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_abs_tt
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
				prev = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_abs_ttt
						value = prev
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = array_get_max_abs_ttt
							var:array_get_max_abs_ttt < 0
						}
						change_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_ttt
							multiply = -1
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							var:array_get_max_abs_tt = { 
								compare_value < prev.var:array_get_max_abs_ttt
							}
						}
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_t
							value = prev
						}
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_tt
							value = var:array_get_max_abs_ttt
						}
						set_global_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_tt
							value = global_var:array_get_max_abs_t
						}
					}
					change_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_abs_t
						add = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_val_0_food
				value = var:array_get_max_abs_t
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_val_0_food
				divide = 10
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_abs_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_abs_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_abs_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_t
			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_tt

			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_rev_0_food
				value = var:toggle_county_commerce_val_0_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_rev_0_food
				multiply = -1
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_0_food
					var:toggle_county_commerce_val_0_food != 0
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = toggle_county_commerce_t
					position = global_var:toggle_county_commerce_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = toggle_county_commerce_scope_0_food
							value = prev
						}
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = toggle_county_commerce_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
					position = global_var:toggle_county_commerce_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_abs_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_abs_tt
				value = 0
			}

						}
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_tt

						set_global_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_tt

						}
					}
					change_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_abs_t

			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_t

			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_tt

				name = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_food
				value = var:toggle_county_commerce_val_2_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_food
				multiply = -1
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_2_food
					var:toggle_county_commerce_val_2_food != 0

				ordered_in_list = {

			clear_variable_list = toggle_county_commerce_t

					scope:toggle_county_commerce_t = {

						set_global_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_abs_tt
							value = global_var:array_get_max_abs_t
						}
					}
					change_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_abs_t
						add = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_val_2_armaments
				value = var:array_get_max_abs_t
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_val_2_armaments
				divide = 10
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_abs_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_abs_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_abs_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_t
			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_abs_ttt
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_armaments
				value = var:toggle_county_commerce_val_2_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_rev_2_armaments
				multiply = -1
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = toggle_county_commerce_val_2_armaments
					var:toggle_county_commerce_val_2_armaments != 0
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = toggle_county_commerce_t
					position = global_var:toggle_county_commerce_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = toggle_county_commerce_scope_2_armaments
							value = prev
						}
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = toggle_county_commerce_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
					position = global_var:toggle_county_commerce_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_global_variable = toggle_county_commerce_t
			clear_variable_list = toggle_county_commerce_t
			clear_variable_list = array_toggle_county_commerce_t
		}
	}
}

					add = var:pop_calorie_actual_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_nutrient_food
					var:pop_nutrient_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_pop_food
					add = var:pop_nutrient_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_nutrient_actual_food
					var:pop_nutrient_actual_food > 0
				}

					var:pop_luxury_actual_armaments > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = toggle_prov_economy_in_pop_armaments
					add = var:pop_luxury_actual_armaments
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = prod_instances
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_sply_old_armaments
						var:prod_sply_old_armaments > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = toggle_prov_economy_sply_armaments
							add = prev.var:prod_sply_old_armaments
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_dmnd_old_armaments
						var:prod_dmnd_old_armaments > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_prod_armaments
							add = prev.var:prod_dmnd_old_armaments
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_in_old_armaments
						var:prod_in_old_armaments > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = toggle_prov_economy_in_prod_armaments
							add = prev.var:prod_in_old_armaments
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = build_slots
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = build_armaments
						var:build_armaments > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_build_armaments
							add = prev.var:build_armaments
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = build_in_armaments
						var:build_in_armaments > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = toggle_prov_economy_in_build_armaments
							add = prev.var:build_in_armaments
						}
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_armaments
				add = var:toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_pop_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_armaments
				add = var:toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_prod_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_armaments
				add = var:toggle_prov_economy_dmnd_build_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_prov_economy_in_armaments
				add = var:toggle_prov_economy_in_pop_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_prov_economy_in_armaments
				add = var:toggle_prov_economy_in_prod_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = toggle_prov_economy_in_armaments
				add = var:toggle_prov_economy_in_build_armaments
			}
		}
	}
}

toggle_prov_pop = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_pop
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_pop
			remove_variable = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
			remove_variable = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
				value = 0
			}
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_pop
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
				value = var:pop_earn_free
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
				add = var:pop_earn_serf
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
				value = var:pop_pay_free
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
				add = var:pop_pay_serf
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						has_variable = extraction_potential
					}
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = extraction_potential
					value = 0
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_farm
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_pasture
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_forest
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_extraction
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_workshop
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
				value = 0
			}

				name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
				value = 0
			}

				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
				value = 0

				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
				value = 0

				value = 0

				value = 0
			}

toggle_prov_prod = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_prod
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_prod
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_prod
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

toggle_prov_merchant = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_merchant
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_merchant
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = trade_merchant
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_merchant
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_in_scope_4_armaments
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = trade_merchant
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_merchant_dat
				value = 1
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = toggle_prov_merchant_dat_t
			var:trade_merchant = { 
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = trade_dat_food
					scope:toggle_prov_merchant_dat_t = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = array_trade_dat_food
					scope:toggle_prov_merchant_dat_t = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = array_toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_tt
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = -210000
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						prev.var:array_get_max_t = { 
							compare_value < prev
						}
					}
					set_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_tt
						value = global_var:array_get_max_t
					}
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_t
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				change_global_variable = { 
					name = array_get_max_t
					add = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_merchant_out_val_0_food
				value = var:array_get_max_t
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_merchant_out_val_0_food
				divide = 10
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_t
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = info_dat_merchant_out_val_0_food
					var:info_dat_merchant_out_val_0_food > 0
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
					position = global_var:toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = info_dat_merchant_out_scope_0_food
							value = prev
						}
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = array_toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
					position = global_var:toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = array_toggled_prov_merchant_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_1_pottery

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_0_tools
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_0_tools

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_1_tools
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_1_tools
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_1_tools

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_2_tools
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_2_tools
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_scope_2_tools

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_0_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_0_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_scope_0_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_1_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_1_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_1_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_scope_1_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_2_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_scope_2_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_2_armaments
			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_scope_2_armaments
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_dat
				value = 1
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = toggle_county_dat
			county = { 
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = trade_dat_food
					scope:toggle_county_dat = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = toggled_county_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = array_trade_dat_food
					scope:toggle_county_dat = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = array_toggled_county_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_tt
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = -210000
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						prev.var:array_get_max_t = { 
							compare_value < prev
						}
					}
					set_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_tt
						value = global_var:array_get_max_t
					}
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_t
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				change_global_variable = { 
					name = array_get_max_t
					add = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_out_val_0_food
				value = var:array_get_max_t
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_out_val_0_food
				divide = 10
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_dat_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_t
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_0_food
					var:info_dat_county_out_val_0_food > 0
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = toggled_county_dat_t
					position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = info_dat_county_out_scope_0_food
							value = prev
						}
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = toggled_county_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
					position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value

				name = info_dat_county_out_val_2_armaments
				divide = 10
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_dat_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_t
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_2_armaments
					var:info_dat_county_out_val_2_armaments > 0
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = toggled_county_dat_t
					position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = info_dat_county_out_scope_2_armaments
							value = prev
						}
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = toggled_county_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
					position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
					prev = { 
						remove_list_variable = { 
							name = array_toggled_county_dat_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = { 
				remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_2_armaments
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_min_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_min_tt
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_min_t
				value = 210000
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						prev.var:array_get_min_t = { 
							compare_value > prev
						}
					}
					set_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_min_tt
						value = global_var:array_get_min_t
					}
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_min_t
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				change_global_variable = { 
					name = array_get_min_t
					add = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_in_val_0_armaments

close_prov_merchant_link = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_merchant_link
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_merchant_link
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_scope_0
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_0
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_scope_1
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_1

			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_2

			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_4

			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_5
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_scope_6
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_6

			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_7
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_scope_8
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_8

			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_link_val_9

toggle_prov_merchant_core = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_merchant_core
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_merchant_core
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_0
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_0
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_1
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_1
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_2
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_2
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_3
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_3
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_4
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_4
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_5
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_5
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_6
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_6
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_7
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_7
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_8
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_8
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_9
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_9
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_10
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_10
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_11
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_11
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_12
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_12
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_13
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_13
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_14
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_14
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_15
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_15
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_16
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_16
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_17
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_17
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_18
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_18
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_19
			remove_variable = info_dat_merchant_core_val_19
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = trade_merchant
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_merchant_core
				value = 0
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
			var:trade_merchant = { 
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = trade_core
					scope:toggle_prov_merchant_core_t = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = array_trade_core
					scope:toggle_prov_merchant_core_t = { 
						add_to_variable_list = { 
							name = array_toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					variable_list_size = { 
						name = toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
						value > 0
					}
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = toggled_prov_merchant_core
					add = 1
				}
				ordered_in_list = { 
					variable = toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
					position = 0
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = info_dat_merchant_core_scope_0
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_variable = { 
					name = array_get_t
					value = 0
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						OR = { 
							NOT = { 
								has_global_variable = array_get_t
							}
							global_var:array_get_t = 0
						}
					}
					ordered_in_list = { 
						variable = array_toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
						position = 0
						prev = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = info_dat_merchant_core_val_0
								value = prev
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = { 
					ordered_in_list = { 
						variable = array_toggle_prov_merchant_core_t
						position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value

					name = mil_maa_recruit_armaments
					value = 0
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						has_variable = mil_maa_maintain_armaments
					}
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = mil_maa_maintain_armaments
					value = 0
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						has_variable = mil_levy_maintain_armaments
					}
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = mil_levy_maintain_armaments
					value = 0
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_maa_recruit_armaments
				value = var:mil_maa_recruit_armaments
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_maa_maintain_armaments
				value = var:mil_maa_maintain_armaments
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_levy_maintain_armaments
				value = var:mil_levy_maintain_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_maa_recruit_armaments
				multiply = 12
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_maa_maintain_armaments
				multiply = 12
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_levy_maintain_armaments
				multiply = 12
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_dmnd_armaments
				value = var:info_player_stockpile_maa_recruit_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_dmnd_armaments
				add = var:info_player_stockpile_maa_maintain_armaments
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_player_stockpile_dmnd_armaments
				add = var:info_player_stockpile_levy_maintain_armaments
			}
		}
	}
}
close_player_stockpile = { 
	scope = character
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_player_stockpile
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_player_stockpile
			remove_variable = info_player_stockpile_maa_recruit_food
			remove_variable = info_player_stockpile_maa_maintain_food

			remove_variable = info_player_stockpile_maa_recruit_exotics_g
